msg:Let me give you a few points: 1. The location of the hotel is a bit remote, but relatively quiet, suitable for older people or taking children on vacation. There is a lake next to it, but most of them are not open due to decoration, and only about 300 meters can be walked. Walkway. 2. The indoor facilities are obviously not suitable for luxury hotels. The TV remote control in the room we booked cannot be used, the small refrigerator is broken, and there are a lot of stains on the sofa in the house. There is even a round table in the place where the desk should be. I don't know what I thought when I was designing it. The trash can in the house is not bagged. I wonder if it is a common problem in Greenland Hotels. 3. There should be some paper towels in the room. I have to call to ask for it. I don't know if the hotel is ready for opening or something. Fourth, the hotel breakfast is not rich, it is not up to the breakfast standard of a five-star hotel, and it is limited to eating full.
The above is a personal check-in experience, you can measure it yourself.

msg:Tucao first. The hotel hasn't been completely renovated yet, and there is only a section of the lakeside trail, which is not connected to the outside world. When I went there, the attitude of welcoming guests was average. I asked where the underground garage was and ignored them. The elevator buttons are unclear, and the front desk can't be found at once. There is a serious smell in the corridors of the guest rooms, and the rooms are slightly better. The front desk staff was not well trained and couldn't answer the questions asked, and forgot to swipe the card. Toiletries need to be picked up at the front desk, but they are not asked when checking in. No one answers the room service calls during certain hours at night, so you need to go downstairs to the front desk yourself. Breakfast is not a buffet, only Chinese and Western set menus can be selected. All trash cans in the room are not covered with trash bags, and I donâ€™t think it is appropriate to throw away some trash. There are only eight kinds of beverages in the refrigerator, and there is a charge. Obviously I am sorry for the price. The rooms at half the price of Wanda are free.
Say something good. The hotel is very clean, and the lake view room can indeed enjoy the entire lake view. Most of the staff are still very enthusiastic, knowing that their hotel is a bit like a maze, and will lead you where you want to go. The variety of breakfast is also okay, at least itâ€™s okay to eat enough, and pay attention to nutrition.
The overall feeling is that the hardware is still good in the future, and the service needs to be improved. I am far from sorry for the price.
